msg:The hotel is in a good location and is a relatively high-end hotel in Yixing.
There is a large parking lot at the door, which is safe and convenient.
The hotel has complete facilities, spacious and comfortable rooms, average breakfast, and a well-equipped gym. Some equipment is damaged and needs to be repaired and replaced in time.
The professional image and service awareness of the hotel's front desk staff need to be improved. In the face of possible busyness during holidays, basic coping measures should be taken.
About 5 kilometers away from the hotel by taxi, there is a "Red Mud Hotel", authentic Jiangsu and Zhejiang cuisine, first-class service awareness, and recommended delicious dishes: steamed white fish, fried eel shreds, with Laoshayouhuang, haha, beautiful and joyful.

msg:Located in the center of Yixing, opposite is the Chengnan River, which connects to a scenic spot. The view is good on the 20th floor, and the bridge is lit at night. You can also walk, which is very good. The overall environment of the hotel is quiet. The family room is suitable for two families. The room is super large and has a small living room. The only drawback is that there is only one bathroom and two toilets. The hotel is close to Shunan Street, and it takes half an hour to drive to other scenic spots. Parking is free. You have to go to breakfast early, otherwise the ingredients will be eaten up. The hotel customer service staff are relatively warm and friendly, and they will solve any problems as soon as possible. If you can't book a hotel in the scenic area, you can try this one

msg:On the eve of the Chinese New Year, my family traveled through Yixing and stayed at Dongyi International Hotel. The hotel is easy to find and parking is convenient. There were not many people during the Chinese New Year. The hotel lobby was very grand and the waiters were very nice. The family room we booked was 60 square meters, very large, and the setting was also very new. The accommodation experience was very comfortable, especially facing Tuanyu Lake, overlooking the entire cherry blossom plank road and the city. The lights were bright and beautiful at night.
